<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> (5)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*na</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂neh₃</i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg/220px-Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg/330px-Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg/440px-Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="3000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пень.html>пне́</a> (a dog on a stump)</div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_4">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">na</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> onto, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> stol</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>onto</b> the table</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вь</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Postávʹ/Položí tarélku <b>na</b> stol.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Put the plate <b>onto</b> the table.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сел</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>стул</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja sel <b>na</b> stul.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've sat <b>on</b> a chair.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> что-то.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nastupíl <b>na</b> što-to.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped <b>on</b> something.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́ну</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nastupíl <b>na</b> mínu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped <b>on</b> a land mine.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случайно.html>случа́йно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>na</b> tebja slučájno nastupíl, izviní.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped on you accidently, sorry.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жвачка.html>жва́чку</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nastupíl <b>na</b> žváčku.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped <b>in</b> gum.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>Твоё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:висеть.html>виси́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючке́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стене́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tvojó palʹtó visít <b>na</b> krjučké <b>na</b> stené.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Your coat is hung <b>on</b> the hook <b>on</b> the wall.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повесить.html>пове́сили</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убийство.html>уби́йство</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne xočú, štóby <b>na</b> menjá povésili ubíjstvo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't want the crime to be pinned <b>on</b> me.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">places, only certain nouns</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> nearby, by (in the sense of near). Interchangable with <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> (which requires genitive case).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реке́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:озеро.html>о́зере</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рой</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>рыб</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My živjóm <b>na</b> móre/reké/ózere, v kotórom/kotóroj/kotórom živjót mnógo ryb.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We live <b>by</b> a sea/river/lake in which many fish live.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to, toward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> póčtu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to the post office</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>ухожу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó, ja uxožu <b>na</b> rabotu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's it, I'm going <b>to</b> work now.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нулся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>се́вер</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:затем.html>зате́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обратно.html>обра́тно</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On dvínulsja <b>na</b> séver, zatém obrátno.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He moved north then back.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:германия.html>герма́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A jésli Germánija dvínetsja <b>na nas</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What if Germany moves towards <b>us</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбо́ры</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U tebjá dve minúty <b>na</b> sbóry.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You have two minutes <b>to</b> pack [your belongings].</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:благотворительный.html>благотвори́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компания.html>компа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:направленный.html>напра́влена</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улучшение.html>улучше́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Náša blagotvorítelʹnaja kompánija naprávlena <b>na</b> ulučšénije míra.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Our charitable organization is aimed <b>to</b> improve the world.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set out for (in the sense "to start an activity with the intention of finishing it"), to go for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иди́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>драко́на</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смочь.html>смо́жешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убить.html>уби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>по́ка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сначала.html>снача́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> квест <a href = vnd.unilang:выполнить.html>вы́полнить</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne idí <b>na</b> étovo drakóna, ty jevó ne smóžešʹ ubítʹ póka, tebé nádo snačála tot kvest výpolnitʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't go <b>for</b> that dragon, you can't kill it for now, you need to complete that other quest first.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладно.html>ла́дно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> прокача́лся <a href = vnd.unilang:достаточно.html>доста́точно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойду́</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:босс.html>бо́сса</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu ládno, ja prokačálsja dostátočno, tak što (pojdú) <b>na</b> glávnovo bóssa sejčás ja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Okay, I've levelled up enough, and now I'm set out <b>for</b> the final boss.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эй.html>Эй</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союзник.html>сою́зник</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ej! Ne nádo <b>na</b> menjá! Ja že tvoj sojúznik.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Hey, don't attack me (don't go <b>after</b> me)! I'm your teammate.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">duration, value, purpose</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> što?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what for?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́чу</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto tebé <b>na</b> udáču!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm giving you this <b>for</b> good luck!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">А-а, дак <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́чу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A-a, dak éto tebé <b>na</b> udáču.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Oh, this is <b>for</b> your luck.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> 500 <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вил</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подведи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>na</b> tebjá 500 rubléj postávil, ne podvedí menjá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've bet 500 roubles <b>on</b> you, don't let me down.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́йте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропитание.html>пропита́ние</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Podájte <b>na</b> propitánije!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give us something (money, food, etc.) <b>to</b> eat!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́таешь</a>? <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> алексе́я?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> kovó rabótaješʹ? <b>Na</b> Alekséja?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Whom do you work <b>for</b>? For Alexey?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> about, for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объявить.html>объяви́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́мму</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On obʺjavíl prográmmu <b>na</b> slédujuščij denʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He announced a program <b>for</b> the next day.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> +accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> over; by; divided by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>Шесть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лится</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Šestʹ délitsja <b>na</b> tri — eto dva.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Six divided <b>by</b> three is two.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лится</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹ <b>na</b> dva ne délitsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five is not divisible <b>by</b> two</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> in, for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> sevódnja vsjó!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's all <b>for</b> today!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> závtra tebe takóje zadánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Here is a task that's ought to be completed by tomorrow.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xóčešʹ ostátʹsja tut <b>na</b> sevódnja?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Would you like to stay here <b>for the rest of</b> the day (i.e. <b>till</b> tomorrow)?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>Придёшь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́лю</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pridjóšʹ na slédujuščuju nedelju?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Will you come for (whole of) the next week?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> in, for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>Придёшь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pridjóšʹ na slédujuščej nedele?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Will you come the next week?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> on, upon

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сижу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>сту́ле</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sižú <b>na</b> stúle.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I sit <b>on</b> a chair.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́не</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On (sidít) <b>na</b> geroíne.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is <b>on</b> heroin.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only with certain nouns</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> in, at
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> póčte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the post office</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́те</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Izviníte, on sejčás <b>na</b> rabóte.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Sorry, he is at work.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́де</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> zavóde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the factory</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>стра́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>краю́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бездна.html>бе́здны</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Strána stoít <b>na</b> krajú bézdny.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The country is <b>at</b> the brink of an abbyss.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">'<i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><b> <a href = vnd.unilang:украина.html>украи́не</a></b></i><b> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"></i></b><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na<b> Ukraíne</b></i><b> ― <span class="e-translation"></span></b>in</i> Ukraine</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> using a means of transport to get somewhere (while <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> is just 'to be in something')
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бусе</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гаем</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My obýčno <b>na</b> avtóbuse, i vot tepérʹ opjátʹ <b>na</b> njóm; sidím v njóm, stoím, inogdá prýgajem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We usually go <b>by</b> bus, and now we've got <b>on</b> it again; here we're sitting, standing, and sometimes jumping.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> runs/operates only because of someone/something; works on, runs on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a> полфи́рмы <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́тся</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da <b>na</b> njóm polfírmy stoít, a to i vsja, ne daj bog s nim što slučítsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Half of the company or even the whole company <b>operates solely thanks to</b> the work he does, god forbid something bad happens to him.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>Их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компания.html>компа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строитель.html>строи́телях</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> — жа́дины — <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сидя́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́слах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>получа́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> бо́льше, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> трюдя́ги.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ix kompánija stoít <b>na</b> stroíteljax, a oní — žádiny — sidját na kréslax svoíx i pri étom polučájut v désjatʹ raz bólʹše, čem trjudjági.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Their company <b>lives only because they have </b> construction workers, nevertheless they—the greedy guys—just sit on their chair, and yet get ten times more money than the sloggers.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электричество.html>электри́честве</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> ко́ка-ко́ле.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dánnyj kompʹjúter rabótajet ne na elektríčestve, a na kóka-kóle.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This computer runs not <b>on</b> electricity, but <b>on</b> cola.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> is assigned to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хня</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́т</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:однако.html>одна́ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хнею</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>поро́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заниматься.html>занима́ется</a> заме́сто <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хотя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>прошу́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> mne (stoít) kúxnja, a <b>na</b> nej (stoját) déti, odnáko i kúxneju oná poróju dáže zanimájetsja zamésto menjá, xotjá jejó tovó i ne prošú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I do the kitchen, while she raises children, yet sometimes she does my work without me asking her for.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дочь.html>дочь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чером</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вернуться.html>верну́сь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> tebé dočʹ mojá, poká ja véčerom ne vernúsʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Look after my daughter until I come back in the evening.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with, for</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism<span class="ib-comma">,</span> +prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> being dominated by a certain emotional state
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвах</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказывать.html>расска́зывай</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́лось</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vsjá <b>na</b> nérvax, rasskázyvaj, štó u tebjá tam slučílosʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm so freaking <b>nervous</b>, tell me what happened to you.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчерашний.html>вчера́шнего</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приставать.html>пристава́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On i tak <b>na</b> nérvax pósle včerášnevo, ne pristaváj k nemú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is already <b>on edge</b> after what happened yesterday, don't bug him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism<span class="ib-comma">,</span> +prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> accomplishing something while being dominated by a certain emotional state <b>and</b> primarily because of it
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неожиданно.html>неожи́данно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подряд.html>подря́д</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охватить.html>охвати́ла</a> дизмора́ль (<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́лась</a> дизмора́ль), <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́е</a> 8 <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neožídanno proigráv tri ráza podrjád, jevo oxvatila dizmorálʹ (u nevó pojavílasʹ dizmorálʹ), i <b>na nej</b> proigrál i vse drugíje 8 raz.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After he had suddenly lost 3 times in a row, he got dismoral, and <b>while being affected by it</b> he lost all the remaining 8 times.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́лись</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достях</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> приоде́вшись, <a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:загс.html>Загс</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жениться.html>жени́ться</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pósle takój dólgoj razlúki, my ne uderžálisʹ, i <b>na rádostjax</b>, dáže kak slédujet ne priodévšisʹ, srázu že pošlí v ZAGS ženítʹsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After such a long separation, <b>thanks to us being so happy</b> we couldn't hold it any longer and went straight to the marriage registrar's office in order to marry, without us even having dressed up appropriately.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сын</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ваш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телевизор.html>телеви́зор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкинуть.html>вы́кинул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:специальный.html>специа́льно</a>… <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:эмоция.html>эмо́циях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:застать.html>заста́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> те́лик — <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́лось</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ponimájete li, syn moj vaš nóvyj televízor výkinul v oknó (iz okná) ne speciálʹno… prósto on byl <b>na</b> emócijax pósle tovó, kak zastál jejó, a télik — on prósto pérvoje, što jemú podvernúlosʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You see, my son threw your new TV set out of the window unintentionally… it's just that he <b>had such an outburst of emotions</b> after having caught her, that he had <b>had to do something</b>, and the first thing that crossed his mind was your new TV set.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набег.html>набе́г</a> (15333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набега́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabegátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набег.html>набе́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabég</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набег.html>набе́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набе́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набег.html>набе́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>incursion, raid, foray <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of barbarians, nomads, gangs, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>surge, rush, gust</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набега́ть</a> (11922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набе́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabégatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover a total <i>(distance)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run <i>(till one is)</i>, to run oneself <i>(to the point of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аппетит.html>аппети́т</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabegatʹ</b> sebé appetít</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to get a good appetite after much running</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одышка.html>оды́шку</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabegatʹ</b> sebé odýšku</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to run till one is short of breath</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набегаться.html>набе́гаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nabegatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run <i>(against)</i>, to dash</li>
<li><i>(waves)</i> to roll in, to coast in</li>
<li>to run <i>(over)</i>, to cover
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́квы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набегают</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>другу́ю</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">búkvy nabegajut odná na drugúju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">letters are running over</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come running <i>(together)</i></li>
<li><i>(liquid)</i> to accumulate <i>(quickly)</i></li>
<li><i>(cloth)</i> to ruck up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набежа́ть</a> (12268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набегать.html>набега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run <i>(against)</i>, to dash</li>
<li><i>(waves)</i> to roll in, to coast in</li>
<li>to run <i>(over)</i>, to cover</li>
<li>to come running <i>(together)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набежа́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́ду</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabežálo</b> mnógo naródu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">people came running up</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(liquid)</i> to accumulate <i>(quickly)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набежа́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>ведро́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">srázu <b>nabežálo</b> pólnoje vedró vody</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the pail was at once brimful of water</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набежать.html>набежа́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лужа.html>лу́жа</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabežála</b> lúža</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a pool formed</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(cloth)</i> to ruck up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набекрень.html>набекре́нь</a> (19429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бекре́нь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bekrénʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набекрень.html>набекре́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabekrénʹ</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a> (9966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набить.html>наби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набить.html>наби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stuff <i>(with)</i>, to pack <i>(with)</i>, to fill <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бку</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabivátʹ</b> trúbku</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to fill one's pipe</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погреб.html>по́греб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>сне́гом</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabivátʹ</b> pógreb snégom</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to pack a cellar with snow</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чучело.html>чу́чело</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тного</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabivátʹ</b> čúčelo živótnovo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to stuff an animal</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nabivátʹ sebé cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enhance one's reputation; make oneself sought after</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nabivátʹ karmány</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to line one's own pockets</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nabivátʹ cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bid up; raise the price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to print</li>
<li>to tap <i>(on)</i>, to fix <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обруч.html>о́бручи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бочку</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabivátʹ</b> obruči na bočku</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to bind a cask with hoops</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подковка.html>подко́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обувь.html>о́бувь</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabivátʹ</b> podkovki na óbuvʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to tap metal tips (on shoes); calk tap (shoes)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to key in</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набиваться.html>набива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набиться.html>наби́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crowd, to be packed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> into or + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to impose oneself on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набиваться.html>набива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabivátʹsja</b> v gósti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invite oneself somewhere</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивший.html>наби́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabívšij</span>)
</p>

***набирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a> (3804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set up, to compose, to type (a text on a computer)</li>
<li>to gather; to pick; to collect; to assemble; to take (a lot of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>грибо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> korzínu gribóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gather a basket of mushrooms</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заказ.html>зака́зов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> zakázov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take a lot of orders</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>у́гля</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угля́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> úglja/ugljá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take on coal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take on; to enlist, to recruit; to engage; to enrol, to make up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> rabóčix na zavód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take on workers at a factory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:учащийся.html>уча́щихся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> učáščixsja v téxnikum</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enrol students (for technical school)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труппа.html>тру́ппу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> trúppu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make up a (e.g. theatre) company</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>idiomatic</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́на</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> nómer (telefóna)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dial a (telephone) number</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:темп.html>те́мпы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹ</b> tɛ́mpy rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to achieve a good pace of work</span></div></dd>

***набираться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a> (11881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather, to accumulate, to come up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to be there</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collect, to summon up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:храбрость.html>хра́брости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹsja</b> xrábrosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pluck/summon up one's courage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹsja</b> dúxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹsja</b> nóvyx sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">summon up fresh energy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наглость.html>на́глости</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> (+ )</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹsja</b> náglosti i (+ )</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take the audacity (+ to )</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to learn, to pick up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опыт.html>о́пыта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabirátʹsja</b> ópyta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gain/accumulate experience</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be full, to tank up <i>(on alcohol)</i>, to load up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***набить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набить.html>наби́ть</a> (6344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набить.html>наби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набивать.html>набива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stuff, to pack, to fill</li>
<li>to fix (onto)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to type (some text)</li>
<li>to break, to smash (a lot of something)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набиться.html>наби́ться</a> (14937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набить.html>наби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набиться.html>наби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набиваться.html>набива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crowd, to be packed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> into or + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to impose oneself on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набиться.html>наби́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabítʹsja</b> v gósti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invite oneself somewhere</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набить.html>наби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдатель.html>наблюда́тель</a> (5598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдать.html>наблюда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabljudátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдатель.html>наблюда́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabljudátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдательный.html>наблюда́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabljudátelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наблюда́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наблюда́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> observation, observational
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдательный.html>наблюда́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пункт.html>пункт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabljudátelʹnyj</b> punkt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">observation post</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>observant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдательный.html>наблюда́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabljudátelʹnyj</b> rebjónok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">observant child</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> supervision, supervisory
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдательный.html>наблюда́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabljudátelʹnyj</b> sovét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">supervisory council</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***наблюдать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдать.html>наблюда́ть</a> (1180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдать.html>наблюда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabljudátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понаблюдать.html>понаблюда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to watch, to observe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдать.html>наблюда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> ке́м-либо/че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabljudátʹ</b> za kém-libo/čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to watch someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to study</li>
<li>to supervise, to take care of</li></ol>

***набор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набор.html>набо́р</a> (3891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набор.html>набо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набор.html>набо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набор.html>набо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набор.html>набо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>set, kit, outfit, collection (collection of various objects for a particular purpose, such as a set of tools)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> font type case containing movable type</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> typesetting, composition</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> typesetting plate</li>
<li>enlistment, admission, levy, recruitment, enrollment</li>
<li>wire gage, gauge</li>
<li>bank of cells</li>
<li>dialing (telephony)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> climb</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наборщик.html>набо́рщик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naborščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
